Market: Armenia | File: bessam-grid.json
  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.en
  Value: ENA (Electric Networks of Armenia) is the main electricity distribution network operator in Armenia, responsible for grid connection of distributed and utility-scale generation and storage assets. The Public Services Regulatory Commission (PSRC) is the sector regulator that sets rules for grid-connected energy installations. All grid-connected BESS installations in Armenia require PSRC-authorised technical review and ENA interconnection approval. Armenia's grid operates at 50 Hz, 220/380 V (same nominal frequency and voltage as China), which reduces the voltage-reconfiguration burden on Chinese BESS power conversion systems (PCS) compared to markets such as Qatar (240/415 V). However, PSRC and ENA define their own protection parameter specifications, communication interface requirements, and technical acceptance criteria — Chinese GB/T grid-connection certificates and NEA approvals are not transferable. Armenia is an EAEU member and EAEU Technical Regulations may impose additional requirements on in-scope BESS equipment. Where project specifications reference IEC 62933 (Electrical Energy Storage Systems) series standards including IEC 62933-2-1 and IEC 62933-5-2, BESS suppliers must prepare documentation accordingly. A publicly accessible PSRC or ENA technical specification document specifically for BESS grid connection had not been confirmed as of the dataset date; project-specific connection terms must be obtained directly from PSRC and ENA.

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.zh
  Value: ENA（亚美尼亚电网公司）是亚美尼亚主要的配电网运营商，负责分布式及公用事业规模发电和储能资产的电网接入。公共服务监管委员会（PSRC）是行业监管机构，制定并网储能装置的规则。亚美尼亚所有并网BESS装置均须取得PSRC授权的技术审查及ENA电网接入许可。亚美尼亚电网运行参数为50 Hz、220/380 V（与中国标称频率和电压相同），这降低了中国BESS储能变流器（PCS）相较于卡塔尔（240/415 V）等市场的电压重新配置负担。但PSRC和ENA有其自身的保护参数规格、通信接口要求和技术验收标准——中国GB/T并网证书和NEA审批不可转用。亚美尼亚是EAEU成员国，EAEU技术法规可能对范围内BESS设备提出额外要求。若项目规格引用IEC 62933（电化学储能系统）系列标准（包括IEC 62933-2-1和IEC 62933-5-2），BESS供应商须相应准备文件。截至本数据集日期，尚未确认PSRC或ENA公开发布专门针对BESS并网的技术规格文件；项目专属并网条款须直接向PSRC和ENA获取。

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.zht
  Value: ENA（亞美尼亞電網公司）是亞美尼亞主要的配電網運營商，負責分布式及公用事業規模發電和儲能資產的電網接入。公共服務監管委員會（PSRC）是行業監管機構，制定併網儲能裝置的規則。亞美尼亞所有併網BESS裝置均須取得PSRC授權的技術審查及ENA電網接入許可。亞美尼亞電網運行參數為50 Hz、220/380 V（與中國標稱頻率和電壓相同），這降低了中國BESS儲能變流器（PCS）相較於卡達（240/415 V）等市場的電壓重新配置負擔。但PSRC和ENA有其自身的保護參數規格、通訊接口要求和技術驗收標準——中國GB/T併網證書和NEA審批不可轉用。亞美尼亞是EAEU成員國，EAEU技術法規可能對範圍內BESS設備提出額外要求。若項目規格引用IEC 62933（電化學儲能系統）系列標準（包括IEC 62933-2-1和IEC 62933-5-2），BESS供應商須相應準備文件。截至本數據集日期，尚未確認PSRC或ENA公開發布專門針對BESS併網的技術規格文件；項目專屬併網條款須直接向PSRC和ENA獲取。

  Path: [0].cn_common_equivalent.summary.en
  Value: China's grid-connection requirements for BESS are governed by GB/T 36558-2023 (General Technical Requirements for Electrochemical Energy Storage Systems in Power Systems) and GB/T 34120-2023 (Technical Specification for Electrochemical Energy Storage System Connected to Distribution Network). The PCS (energy storage converter) is assessed under NB/T 42090-2016 (Technical Code for Testing of Energy Storage Converters). Chinese BESS products are validated by grid operators through National Energy Administration (NEA)-authorised procedures. China's grid operates at 50 Hz, 220/380 V — the same nominal values as Armenia, which means no voltage level re-parameterisation is required at the grid interface level. However, PSRC and ENA protection relay settings, anti-islanding requirements, and SCADA/communication protocol specifications are independent of Chinese NEA approvals and must be met separately.

  Path: [0].cn_common_equivalent.summary.zh
  Value: 中国BESS并网要求由GB/T 36558-2023（电力系统电化学储能系统通用技术条件）和GB/T 34120-2023（电化学储能系统接入配电网技术规范）管控。储能变流器（PCS）依据NB/T 42090-2016（储能变流器检测技术规程）进行评估。中国BESS产品通过国家能源局（NEA）授权程序获得电网运营商认可。中国电网运行参数为50 Hz、220/380 V——与亚美尼亚标称值相同，意味着电网接口层面无需进行电压等级重新参数配置。但PSRC和ENA的继电保护整定值、防孤岛要求及SCADA/通信协议规格独立于中国NEA审批，须另行满足。

  Path: [0].cn_common_equivalent.summary.zht
  Value: 中國BESS併網要求由GB/T 36558-2023（電力系統電化學儲能系統通用技術條件）和GB/T 34120-2023（電化學儲能系統接入配電網技術規範）管控。儲能變流器（PCS）依據NB/T 42090-2016（儲能變流器檢測技術規程）進行評估。中國BESS產品通過國家能源局（NEA）授權程序獲得電網運營商認可。中國電網運行參數為50 Hz、220/380 V——與亞美尼亞標稱值相同，意味著電網接口層面無需進行電壓等級重新參數配置。但PSRC和ENA的繼電保護整定值、防孤島要求及SCADA/通訊協議規格獨立於中國NEA審批，須另行滿足。

  Path: [0].gap.en
  Value: Gap: Chinese GB/T BESS grid-connection certificates and NEA approvals do not satisfy PSRC/ENA grid-connection requirements in Armenia. Key considerations: (a) grid voltage and frequency — Armenia and China share the same 50 Hz, 220/380 V nominal values, reducing voltage-reconfiguration burden; however, PSRC/ENA-specific protection relay settings, anti-islanding parameters, and ride-through thresholds must be verified and configured to Armenian specifications; (b) PSRC and ENA project-specific connection agreement terms — engage PSRC and ENA at the earliest project stage to obtain technical requirements before equipment design is finalised; (c) IEC 62933 series compliance — where project specifications require IEC 62933-2-1 or IEC 62933-5-2 evidence, prepare test and design documentation accordingly; Chinese GB/T standards are not accepted as equivalent; (d) EAEU compliance — where in-scope under EAEU TR CU 004/2011 (LVD) or TR CU 020/2011 (EMC), EAC certification from an EAEU-accredited certification body is required for the BESS equipment; Chinese GB certifications are not accepted; (e) communication protocols — confirm the SCADA/communication interface protocol required by ENA for BESS monitoring (IEC 61850, Modbus, or project-specific specification); (f) renewable integration context — Armenia's grid is experiencing solar growth and PSRC may impose specific grid-support requirements (frequency response, reactive power) for storage assets.

  Path: [0].gap.zh
  Value: 差距：中国GB/T BESS并网证书和NEA审批不满足亚美尼亚PSRC/ENA并网要求。主要注意事项：（a）电网电压和频率——亚美尼亚与中国共享相同的50 Hz、220/380 V标称值，降低了电压重新配置负担；但PSRC/ENA专属继电保护整定值、防孤岛参数和穿越阈值须按亚美尼亚规格核实和配置；（b）PSRC和ENA项目专属并网协议条款——在设备设计最终确定前，应在项目最早阶段与PSRC和ENA接触以获取技术要求；（c）IEC 62933系列合规——若项目规格要求IEC 62933-2-1或IEC 62933-5-2证据，须相应准备测试和设计文件；中国GB/T标准不被接受为等效依据；（d）EAEU合规——若BESS设备属于EAEU TR CU 004/2011（低压设备）或TR CU 020/2011（电磁兼容）范围，须由EAEU认可认证机构颁发EAC证书；中国GB认证不被接受；（e）通信协议——确认ENA对BESS监控所要求的SCADA/通信接口协议（IEC 61850、Modbus或项目专属规格）；（f）可再生能源并网背景——亚美尼亚电网正经历太阳能增长，PSRC可能对储能资产提出具体电网支撑要求（频率响应、无功功率）。

  Value: [INFORMATIONAL] Chinese GB/T BESS grid-connection compliance and NEA approvals do not satisfy PSRC/ENA Armenia grid-connection requirements. Armenia and China share the same 50 Hz, 220/380 V nominal grid parameters, reducing voltage-level reconfiguration burden; however, PSRC/ENA protection settings, anti-islanding requirements, and SCADA/communication specifications must be met independently. Type: EAC_IN_NON_EAEU
Market: Georgia | File: bessge-fire.json
  Path: [0].gap.en
  Value: Gap: Georgian local fire and building authorities require fire-safety design approval and installation permits before BESS commissioning. Chinese BESS fire-safety documentation based on GB standards is not accepted as equivalent to IEC/EN-based requirements under Georgia's DCFTA alignment trajectory. No dedicated Georgian technical regulation specifically for stationary BESS fire safety has been confirmed as of the dataset date — this is a high-priority gap. Exporters and project teams should: (a) engage the relevant Georgian local fire authority and building permit authority at the earliest project stage to confirm applicable fire-safety standards and the approval pathway; (b) prepare BESS fire-safety design documentation aligned with IEC 62933-5-1 and IEC 62619 — including thermal-runaway propagation mitigation, gas detection or ventilation design, suppression system design, emergency shutdown procedures, and separation distances; (c) engage a locally licensed fire protection engineer or safety consultant familiar with Georgian building and fire codes; (d) do NOT assume EAC/TR CU or GOST-R fire-safety certificates are relevant — Georgia is not an EAEU member and such certificates are not recognised.

  Path: [0].gap.zh
  Value: 差距：格鲁吉亚地方消防及建筑主管机关在BESS投运前须批准消防安全设计并颁发安装许可证。依据GB标准编制的中国BESS消防安全文件在格鲁吉亚DCFTA对接轨迹下不被接受为与IEC/EN要求等效。截至本数据集日期，尚未确认格鲁吉亚发布专门针对固定式BESS消防安全的技术法规——这是一个高优先级差距。出口商和项目团队应：（a）在项目最早阶段与格鲁吉亚相关地方消防主管机关和建筑许可主管机关接触，确认适用消防安全标准和审批路径；（b）准备符合IEC 62933-5-1和IEC 62619的BESS消防安全设计文件——包括热失控蔓延缓解、气体探测或通风设计、抑制系统设计、紧急停机程序及隔离距离；（c）聘请熟悉格鲁吉亚建筑和消防规范的持牌本地消防工程师或安全顾问；（d）不得假设EAC/TR CU或GOST-R消防安全证书具有相关性——格鲁吉亚非欧亚经济联盟成员，此类证书不被认可。

  Path: [0].compliance_verdict.en
  Value: [INFORMATIONAL] Local fire and building authority approval is a mandatory installation gate for commercial and industrial BESS in Georgia. Chinese GB-standard fire-safety documentation does not satisfy Georgia's IEC/EN-aligned requirements. Engage the relevant Georgian fire and building authority and a locally licensed fire protection engineer at the earliest project stage to confirm the applicable fire-safety standard (IEC 62933-5-1 / IEC 62619 baseline expected) and design approval requirements before committing to system layout or equipment specification. Do not rely on EAC/TR CU or GOST-R certificates — not applicable in Georgia.

  Value: [仅供参考] 地方消防及建筑主管机关审批是格鲁吉亚商业及工业BESS装置的强制安装门槛。中国GB标准消防安全文件不满足格鲁吉亚IEC/EN对接要求。在确定系统布局或设备规格前，应在项目最早阶段与相关格鲁吉亚消防及建筑主管机关及持牌本地消防工程师接触，确认适用消防安全标准（预期基准为IEC 62933-5-1 / IEC 62619）及设计审批要求。请勿依赖EAC/TR CU或GOST-R证书——在格鲁吉亚不适用。

  Value: Gap: Chinese GB/T BESS grid-connection certificates and NEA approvals do not satisfy GNERC licensing requirements or GSE/distribution-operator grid-connection technical requirements in Georgia. Key points requiring attention: (a) GNERC licence — determine the applicable licence category for BESS (generation licence, storage authorisation, or other) before project development commences; (b) grid-connection agreement — engage GSE (transmission-connected) or Telasi/Energo-Pro Georgia (distribution-connected) at the earliest project stage to obtain technical interface requirements; (c) grid voltage parity — Georgia's 220/380 V grid matches China's nominal voltage, reducing PCS voltage re-parameterisation risk; however, frequency response, reactive power, protection relay settings, and SCADA/communication protocol (IEC 61850, DNP3, or project-specific) must still be confirmed with the grid/distribution operator; (d) IEC 62933 evidence — where project or grid-operator specifications reference IEC 62933-2-1 or IEC 62933-5-2, prepare test and design documentation accordingly; Chinese GB/T standards are not accepted as equivalent under Georgia's IEC/EN alignment framework; (e) do NOT pursue EAC/TR CU (EAEU) certification as the conformity route — Georgia is not an EAEU member and EAC marks are not recognised.

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.en
  Value: GNERC (Georgian National Energy and Water Supply Regulatory Commission) is the independent energy sector regulator in Georgia and issues licences for electricity generation, transmission, distribution, and supply. GSE (Georgian State Electrosystem) is the state-owned transmission system operator responsible for the 220 kV and 500 kV backbone. Distribution is provided by Telasi (Tbilisi area, owned by Tبilisi Energy) and Energo-Pro Georgia (rest of the country). All grid-connected BESS installations require GNERC licensing (as generation or storage, depending on project classification) and a formal grid-connection agreement with GSE (for transmission-connected projects) or the relevant distribution operator (for distribution-connected projects). Georgia's grid operates at 220/380 V, 50 Hz — the same nominal voltage as China's grid — which reduces PCS voltage re-parameterisation requirements relative to markets such as Qatar (240/415 V). However, project-specific frequency response, reactive power, and ride-through requirements must be confirmed with GSE or the distribution operator. IEC 62933 series (Electrical Energy Storage Systems) is the internationally expected technical reference for BESS system-level parameters and is expected to be referenced in project-owner and grid-operator specifications given Georgia's IEC/EN alignment trajectory under DCFTA. Georgia's grid is hydro-dominant with significant seasonal and import dependence; storage is emerging as a balancing and renewable integration technology. A publicly accessible GNERC or GSE technical specification document specifically for BESS grid connection had not been confirmed from official sources as of the dataset date; project-specific requirements must be obtained directly from GNERC and GSE or the relevant distribution operator.

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.zh
  Value: GNERC（格鲁吉亚国家能源和供水监管委员会）是格鲁吉亚独立能源行业监管机构，负责颁发电力发电、输电、配电和供电许可证。GSE（格鲁吉亚国家电力系统）是国有输电系统运营商，负责220 kV和500 kV主干网。配电由Telasi（第比利斯地区）和Energo-Pro Georgia（其余地区）负责。所有并网BESS装置均须取得GNERC许可证（根据项目分类作为发电或储能）及与GSE（输电接入项目）或相关配电运营商（配电接入项目）签订正式并网协议。格鲁吉亚电网运行参数为220/380 V、50 Hz——与中国电网额定电压相同——相对于卡塔尔等市场（240/415 V），降低了储能变流器电压重新配置要求。然而，项目专属频率响应、无功功率和低电压穿越要求仍须与GSE或配电运营商确认。IEC 62933系列（电化学储能系统）是BESS系统级参数的国际预期技术参考，鉴于格鲁吉亚在DCFTA框架下的IEC/EN对接轨迹，预计将在项目业主和电网运营商规格中被引用。格鲁吉亚电网以水电为主，季节性和进口依赖度较高；储能正在成为调频和可再生能源整合技术。截至本数据集日期，尚未从官方来源确认GNERC或GSE公开发布专门针对BESS并网的技术规格文件；项目专属要求须直接向GNERC及GSE或相关配电运营商获取。

  Value: GNERC（喬治亞國家能源和供水監管委員會）是喬治亞獨立能源行業監管機構，負責頒發電力發電、輸電、配電和供電許可證。GSE（喬治亞國家電力系統）是國有輸電系統運營商，負責220 kV和500 kV主幹網。配電由Telasi（第比利斯地區）和Energo-Pro Georgia（其餘地區）負責。所有併網BESS裝置均須取得GNERC許可證（根據項目分類作為發電或儲能）及與GSE（輸電接入項目）或相關配電運營商（配電接入項目）簽訂正式併網協議。喬治亞電網運行參數為220/380 V、50 Hz——與中國電網額定電壓相同——相對於卡達等市場（240/415 V），降低了儲能變流器電壓重新配置要求。然而，項目專屬頻率響應、無功功率和低電壓穿越要求仍須與GSE或配電運營商確認。IEC 62933系列（電化學儲能系統）是BESS系統級參數的國際預期技術參考，鑑於喬治亞在DCFTA框架下的IEC/EN對接軌跡，預計將在項目業主和電網運營商規格中被引用。喬治亞電網以水電為主，季節性和進口依賴度較高；儲能正在成為調頻和可再生能源整合技術。截至本數據集日期，尚未從官方來源確認GNERC或GSE公開發布專門針對BESS併網的技術規格文件；項目專屬要求須直接向GNERC及GSE或相關配電運營商獲取。

  Path: [0].cn_common_equivalent.summary.en
  Value: China's grid-connection requirements for BESS are governed by GB/T 36558-2023 (General Technical Requirements for Electrochemical Energy Storage Systems in Power Systems) and GB/T 34120-2023 (Technical Specification for Electrochemical Energy Storage System Connected to Distribution Network). The PCS (energy storage converter) is assessed under NB/T 42090-2016 (Technical Code for Testing of Energy Storage Converters). Chinese BESS products are validated by grid operators through National Energy Administration (NEA)-authorised procedures. China's grid operates at 50 Hz, 220/380 V (220 V single-phase, 380 V three-phase) — the same nominal voltage as Georgia — which means PCS voltage protection thresholds do not require fundamental re-parameterisation for the Georgia market, unlike higher-voltage markets. However, specific frequency response, reactive power injection, and grid-protection relay settings must still be confirmed against GNERC/GSE/distribution-operator requirements and are not satisfied by Chinese NEA approval alone.

  Value: 中国BESS并网要求由GB/T 36558-2023（电力系统电化学储能系统通用技术条件）和GB/T 34120-2023（电化学储能系统接入配电网技术规范）管控。储能变流器（PCS）依据NB/T 42090-2016（储能变流器检测技术规程）进行评估。中国BESS产品通过国家能源局（NEA）授权程序获得电网运营商认可。中国电网运行参数为50 Hz、220/380 V（单相220 V、三相380 V）——与格鲁吉亚额定电压相同——这意味着PCS电压保护阈值无需像高电压市场那样进行根本性重新配置。然而，特定频率响应、无功功率注入和电网保护继电器设置仍须与GNERC/GSE/配电运营商要求进行确认，仅凭中国NEA审批不足以满足要求。

Type: EAC_IN_NON_EAEU
Market: Georgia | File: bessge-safety.json
  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.en
  Value: Georgia does not currently have a confirmed standalone mandatory BESS product safety regulation equivalent to the EU Battery Regulation or comparable mandatory certification regimes. GEOSTM (Georgian National Agency for Standards and Metrology) is the national standards body responsible for adopting Georgian standards (GOST) and — under Georgia's EU Deep and Comprehensive Free Trade Area (DCFTA) alignment trajectory — progressively adopting IEC and EN international standards. Georgia is NOT an EAEU member; EAC/TR CU (Eurasian Conformity) certification is therefore not the applicable conformity route and EAC marks are not recognised in Georgia. IEC 62619:2022 (Safety Requirements for Secondary Lithium Cells and Batteries for Use in Industrial Applications) is the internationally expected safety standard for lithium BESS cells and modules, and IEC 62133 (Safety Requirements for Portable Sealed Secondary Lithium Cells and Batteries) is referenced for smaller cell formats. Under Georgia's IEC/EN alignment trajectory, project owners, EPCs, and grid operators are expected to reference IEC 62619 compliance as the technical prerequisite for BESS cell and module safety in project specifications. IEC 62933-5-2 (Safety Requirements for Electrochemical-based Energy Storage Systems) is the expected system-level safety reference. Exporters should verify the current GEOSTM adopted-standards list and any mandatory technical regulation scope directly with GEOSTM before shipment.

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.en
  Value: Kyrgyzstan's electricity sector is regulated by the Ministry of Energy and overseen operationally by the National Energy Holding Company (NEHC) and its distribution subsidiaries (Severelectro, Vostokelektro, Oshelectro, Jalalabadelektro). All grid-connected BESS installations require technical review and grid-connection approval from the relevant grid operator. Kyrgyzstan's grid operates at 220/380 V 50 Hz (single-phase 220 V, three-phase 380 V) — the same nominal parameters as China — which reduces PCS voltage reconfiguration risk compared with markets using different voltage standards. However, Kyrgyzstan's grid is characterised by significant seasonal variation: hydro-dominant generation creates summer surplus and pronounced winter energy deficits, and grid stability and frequency quality in rural and mountainous areas may differ from urban centres. BESS project specifications in Kyrgyzstan typically reference IEC 62933 series standards (IEC 62933-2-1 unit parameters; IEC 62933-5-2 safety requirements) where international financing or EPC contractors are involved. A publicly accessible NEHC or Ministry of Energy technical specification document specifically for BESS grid connection had not been confirmed as of the dataset date; project-specific connection agreement terms must be obtained directly from the relevant grid operator. Cold-climate and high-altitude design factors (see besskg-safety) affect PCS operating range and must be addressed in equipment specifications.

  Value: China's grid-connection requirements for BESS are governed by GB/T 36558-2023 (General Technical Requirements for Electrochemical Energy Storage Systems in Power Systems) and GB/T 34120-2023 (Technical Specification for Electrochemical Energy Storage System Connected to Distribution Network). The PCS (energy storage converter) is assessed under NB/T 42090-2016 (Technical Code for Testing of Energy Storage Converters). Chinese BESS products are validated by grid operators through National Energy Administration (NEA)-authorised procedures. China's grid operates at 50 Hz, 220/380 V — the same nominal voltage as Kyrgyzstan — which means PCS voltage protection thresholds and ride-through settings designed for China do not require fundamental re-parameterisation for Kyrgyzstan's grid voltage. However, project-specific grid-quality parameters (frequency stability, harmonic limits, fault-ride-through requirements) must be confirmed with NEHC for each project.

Key considerations: (a) grid voltage parity — Kyrgyzstan and China share the same 220/380 V 50 Hz nominal parameters, so fundamental PCS voltage reconfiguration is not required; however, actual grid-quality conditions (frequency deviation, harmonics, fault levels) in Kyrgyzstan's hydro-dominated and mountainous grid may differ from Chinese grid assumptions embedded in PCS protection firmware — verify with NEHC; (b) NEHC project-specific connection agreement — engage the relevant distribution operator (Severelectro for Bishkek and northern areas, etc.) at the earliest project stage; (c) IEC 62933 series compliance — where project specifications require IEC 62933-2-1 or IEC 62933-5-2 evidence (expected for internationally financed projects), prepare test and design documentation accordingly; Chinese GB/T standards are not accepted as equivalent; (d) EAEU TR CU 004/2011 EAC certification — BESS PCS inverters as low-voltage electrical equipment may be in scope for TR CU 004/2011 mandatory EAC certification before sale in Kyrgyzstan as an EAEU member; verify scope with an EAEU-accredited certification body; (e) cold-climate and high-altitude derating — PCS must be rated for Kyrgyzstan's operating temperature range and, for high-altitude sites, derated or specifically rated for altitude-related effects on cooling and component performance.

  Value: Barqi Tojik (Open Joint Stock Holding Company Barqi Tojik) is Tajikistan's state-owned vertically-integrated electricity utility and the primary grid operator, under the Ministry of Energy and Water Resources of the Republic of Tajikistan. All grid-connected BESS installations — including utility-scale solar-plus-storage projects and behind-the-meter installations — require Barqi Tojik technical approval and connection agreement. Tajikistan's grid operates at 50 Hz (220 V single-phase, 380 V three-phase at the low-voltage distribution level), the same nominal frequency as China, but grid stability characteristics differ: the national grid is predominantly hydropower-dependent (~95% of generation), resulting in severe seasonal output variation and winter energy deficits that create intermittency and frequency excursion risk. BESS power conversion systems (PCS) must be validated for Tajikistan's 50 Hz grid, including frequency ride-through and voltage protection settings appropriate for a hydropower-dominated grid with limited spinning reserve. Donor-funded BESS projects (World Bank, ADB, EBRD) typically incorporate IEC 62933-2-1 and IEC 62933-5-2 requirements into technical specifications. A publicly accessible Barqi Tojik technical specification document specifically for BESS grid connection has not been confirmed as of the dataset date; project-specific connection terms must be obtained directly from Barqi Tojik and coordinating donor/lender technical advisors.

The PCS (energy storage converter) is assessed under NB/T 42090-2016 (Technical Code for Testing of Energy Storage Converters). Chinese BESS products are validated by grid operators through National Energy Administration (NEA)-authorised procedures. China's grid also operates at 50 Hz with 220 V single-phase and 380 V three-phase at the distribution level, matching Tajikistan's nominal voltage — unlike the Qatar 240/415 V difference. However, grid protection settings, frequency ride-through tolerances, and SCADA/communication protocol requirements in Tajikistan are project-specific and may differ from Chinese NEA-standard parameters, particularly for high-altitude deployments above 2,000 m where derating and insulation specifications diverge.

Type: EAC_IN_NON_EAEU
Market: Tajikistan | File: besstj-safety.json
  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.en
  Value: The Tajikistan Committee on Standards, Metrology and Trade (Tajikstandart) under the Ministry of Economic Development and Trade of the Republic of Tajikistan is the national standards and conformity assessment authority. Tajikstandart issues Tajikistan certificates of conformity (Сертификат соответствия) for products on the mandatory certification list, adopting or adapting IEC and GOST standards. CRITICAL NOTE: Tajikistan is NOT a member of the Eurasian Economic Union (EAEU). It holds observer/candidate status only. EAC marks (Eurasian Conformity) and TR CU Technical Regulations — used in Armenia, Belarus, Kazakhstan, Kyrgyzstan, and Russia — do NOT by themselves constitute market access authorisation in Tajikistan. A product with an EAC mark still requires separate Tajikstandart conformity assessment before it can be legally sold or installed in Tajikistan. No confirmed mandatory Tajikstandart Technical Regulation (TR TJ) specifically for stationary lithium BESS products has been identified from publicly accessible official sources as of the dataset date. In practice, donor-funded BESS projects (World Bank, ADB, EBRD) in Tajikistan require IEC 62619 (Safety Requirements for Secondary Lithium Cells and Batteries for Use in Industrial Applications) as the cell and module safety baseline in technical specifications, and IEC 62133 where consumer-grade cells are in scope. Tajikstandart conformity certification plus IEC 62619 evidence is the practical dual gate for BESS market access in Tajikistan.

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.zh
  Value: 塔吉克斯坦共和国经济发展和贸易部下属标准、计量和贸易委员会（Tajikstandart）是国家标准和合格评定主管机关。Tajikstandart为强制认证清单上的产品颁发塔吉克斯坦合格证书（Сертификат соответствия），采纳或改编IEC和GOST标准。重要提示：塔吉克斯坦非欧亚经济联盟（EAEU）成员，仅持有观察员/候选国身份。亚美尼亚、白俄罗斯、哈萨克斯坦、吉尔吉斯斯坦和俄罗斯使用的EAC标志（欧亚合格认证）和TR CU技术法规，本身不构成在塔吉克斯坦的市场准入授权。持有EAC标志的产品在塔吉克斯坦合法销售或安装前，仍须单独进行Tajikstandart合格评定。截至本数据集日期，尚未从可公开获取的官方来源发现专门针对固定式锂BESS产品的已确认强制性Tajikstandart技术法规（TR TJ）。实践中，塔吉克斯坦捐助方资助的BESS项目（世界银行、亚行、欧洲复兴开发银行）在技术规格中要求以IEC 62619（工业应用二次锂电芯和电池安全要求）作为电芯和模组安全基准，消费级电芯适用范围内还引用IEC 62133。Tajikstandart合格认证加IEC 62619证据是塔吉克斯坦BESS市场准入的实际双重门槛。

  Path: [0].cn_common_equivalent.summary.en
  Value: China's primary mandatory standard for BESS cells from August 2025 is GB 44240-2024 (Secondary Lithium Cells and Batteries Used in Electrical Energy Storage Systems — Safety Requirements), replacing the prior GB/T 36276 series as the mandatory safety baseline for large-format BESS batteries over 100 kWh. The prior voluntary standard GB/T 36276-2023 (Lithium-Ion Batteries for Electrical Energy Storage) provides the technical framework for cells, modules, and battery clusters. These Chinese standards are not accepted as equivalents to IEC 62619 in Tajikstandart conformity assessment or donor-funded project specifications. Exporters must obtain IEC 62619 type-test certificates from an ILAC-accredited laboratory and apply for Tajikstandart conformity certification separately from Chinese GB compliance. An EAC certificate (even where held from a neighbouring EAEU market) does not remove the Tajikstandart conformity obligation.

  Path: [0].cn_common_equivalent.summary.zh
  Value: 自2025年8月起，中国BESS电芯的主要强制性标准为GB 44240-2024（电化学储能系统用二次锂电池安全要求），取代原GB/T 36276系列，成为100 kWh以上大型BESS电池的强制性安全基准。此前的自愿性标准GB/T 36276-2023（电力储能用锂离子电池）为EES中使用的电芯、模组和电池簇提供技术框架。上述中国标准不被Tajikstandart合格评定或捐助方资助项目规格接受为IEC 62619的等效依据。出口商须从ILAC认可实验室取得IEC 62619型式试验证书，并独立于中国GB合规申请Tajikstandart合格认证。即使持有相邻EAEU市场的EAC证书，也不免除Tajikstandart合格认证义务。

Type: EAC_IN_NON_EAEU
Market: Georgia | File: evge-market.json
  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.en
  Value: GEOSTM (Georgian National Agency for Standards and Metrology) is Georgia's national standardization body. Georgia's EU DCFTA (Deep and Comprehensive Free Trade Area) obligations commit Georgia to approximate its technical regulations and conformity assessment procedures to EU norms, directing Georgian standards toward IEC/EN frameworks. GEOSTM adopts IEC and EN standards as Georgian standards (GOST-compatible adoption nomenclature is used for legacy reasons, but the direction is EU-aligned, not EAEU). Electrical products imported into Georgia, including EV chargers, may be subject to GEOSTM conformity assessment where technical regulations are in force. As of 2026-06-14, a single published mandatory whole-unit EVSE product certification regulation from GEOSTM could not be confirmed from official sources; exporters should verify the current GEOSTM scope, applicable technical regulation, HS code, and conformity assessment route with GEOSTM or an accredited conformity assessment body before shipment. Georgia is NOT a member of the EAEU — the EAC/TR CU conformity mark route does not apply and must not be claimed.

Type: GRID_DIFFERENCE
Market: Tajikistan | File: evtj-grid.json
  Path: [0].requirement_topic.en
  Value: Barqi Tojik Grid Connection — 220 / 380 V / 50 Hz and Severe Winter Power Deficit

  Path: [0].requirement_topic.zh
  Value: Barqi Tojik并网接入——220/380 V / 50 Hz及严重冬季电力短缺

  Path: [0].requirement_topic.zht
  Value: Barqi Tojik併網接入——220/380 V / 50 Hz及嚴重冬季電力短缺

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.en
  Value: Tajikistan operates on a 220 V single-phase / 380 V three-phase, 50 Hz grid, distributed and regulated by Barqi Tojik (the state electricity utility). Any grid-connected EV charger installation requires coordination with and approval from Barqi Tojik, including supply capacity review, metering, and connection documentation. A structurally important constraint is Tajikistan's severe winter electricity deficit: the country is a net electricity exporter in summer (hydropower surplus from Nurek and Rogun dams) but experiences significant supply shortfalls in winter, with daily power cuts of several hours in residential and commercial areas during peak winter months (typically December–February). This deficit materially constrains the deployment and utilisation of public EV charging infrastructure, particularly DC fast chargers with high peak demand. Grid voltage fluctuation and supply interruption resilience should be designed into the charger. High-altitude installations (Dushanbe at ~750 m; Khujand at ~310 m; mountain routes up to 4,000+ m) impose altitude derating requirements on power electronics cooling.

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.zh
  Value: 塔吉克斯坦采用220 V单相 / 380 V三相、50 Hz电网，由国家电力公司Barqi Tojik配电及监管。任何并网电动汽车充电桩安装须经Barqi Tojik协调和审批，包括供电容量审查、计量和接入文件。一项结构性限制是塔吉克斯坦严重的冬季电力短缺：该国夏季为净电力出口国（努列克和罗贡水坝的水电盈余），但冬季面临明显电力供应短缺，冬季高峰期（通常为12月至2月）住宅和商业区每日断电数小时。这一短缺从根本上制约了公共电动汽车充电基础设施的部署和利用，尤其是峰值需求较高的直流快充桩。充电桩应设计具备电网电压波动和供电中断韧性。高海拔安装（杜尚别约750米；苦盏约310米；山区路线海拔4000米以上）对电力电子冷却系统提出了海拔降额要求。

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.zht
  Value: 塔吉克斯坦採用220 V單相 / 380 V三相、50 Hz電網，由國家電力公司Barqi Tojik配電及監管。任何併網電動汽車充電樁安裝須經Barqi Tojik協調和審批，包括供電容量審查、計量和接入文件。一項結構性限制是塔吉克斯坦嚴重的冬季電力短缺：該國夏季為淨電力出口國（努列克和羅貢水壩的水電盈餘），但冬季面臨明顯電力供應短缺，冬季高峰期（通常為12月至2月）住宅和商業區每日斷電數小時。這一短缺從根本上制約了公共電動汽車充電基礎設施的部署和利用，尤其是峰值需求較高的直流快充樁。充電樁應設計具備電網電壓波動和供電中斷韌性。高海拔安裝（杜尚別約750米；苦盞約310米；山區路線海拔4000米以上）對電力電子冷卻系統提出了高海拔降額要求。

  Path: [0].gap.en
  Value: Exporters must address: (1) Barqi Tojik grid-connection approval — including supply capacity review, metering, and installation documentation; (2) cold-climate rating for charger enclosure, power electronics, and cabling, covering operation at sustained temperatures down to at least −25 °C and storage to −40 °C in mountain regions; (3) high-altitude derating of power electronics cooling (IEC 60664-1 / IEC 60068-2-13 altitude test); (4) input-voltage tolerance design covering Tajikistan grid fluctuations beyond the nominal 220/380 V; (5) UPS or battery buffer strategy if the operator requires charging continuity through power-cut windows; (6) honest communication to the end-customer that winter electricity deficits will reduce charger availability, particularly in Dushanbe and other grid-constrained areas. A standard China domestic charger shipped without cold-climate and altitude validation is likely to fail in Tajikistan mountain conditions.

Type: EAC_IN_NON_EAEU
Market: Tajikistan | File: evtj-market.json
  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.en
  Value: Tajikstandart (the Agency for Standardization, Metrology, Certification and Trade Inspection of the Republic of Tajikistan) administers the national conformity assessment system for Tajikistan. Electrical equipment imported into Tajikistan requires conformity with applicable Tajikstandart-registered standards, evidenced by a conformity certificate or declaration of conformity issued through the Tajikstandart system or an accredited testing and certification body recognised by Tajikstandart. Tajikstandart progressively adopts GOST-R-derived standards and aligns with IEC international standards; the exact applicable standard for EV chargers should be confirmed directly with Tajikstandart or a recognized conformity body, as Tajikistan's EV-specific standard catalogue is limited given the nascent state of the EV market. CRITICAL CLARIFICATION — NOT EAEU: Tajikistan is not a member of the Eurasian Economic Union (EAEU). EAC (Eurasian Conformity) certificates and the TR CU (Technical Regulation of the Customs Union) route are mandatory for EAEU member states (Russia, Kazakhstan, Kyrgyzstan, Armenia, Belarus) but do NOT automatically confer market access in Tajikistan. An EAC mark does not satisfy Tajikstandart requirements. Exporters holding EAC certificates for neighbouring EAEU markets must obtain separate Tajikstandart conformity before exporting to Tajikistan.

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.zh
  Value: Tajikstandart（塔吉克斯坦共和国标准化、计量、认证和贸易检验局）管理塔吉克斯坦国家合格评定体系。进口至塔吉克斯坦的电气设备须符合适用的Tajikstandart注册标准，并须通过Tajikstandart体系或Tajikstandart认可的检测和认证机构签发合格证书或合格声明。Tajikstandart逐步采纳GOST-R衍生标准并与IEC国际标准接轨；电动汽车充电桩适用的具体标准应直接向Tajikstandart或认可合格评定机构确认，因塔吉克斯坦电动汽车特定标准目录受限于市场初期阶段而较为有限。重要说明——非EAEU：塔吉克斯坦不是欧亚经济联盟（EAEU）成员。EAC（欧亚合格评定）证书和TR CU（海关联盟技术法规）路径是EAEU成员国（俄罗斯、哈萨克斯坦、吉尔吉斯斯坦、亚美尼亚、白俄罗斯）的强制路径，但不自动赋予在塔吉克斯坦的市场准入资格。EAC标志不满足Tajikstandart要求。持有邻近EAEU市场EAC证书的出口商，在向塔吉克斯坦出口前须单独获得Tajikstandart合格评定。

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.zht
  Value: Tajikstandart（塔吉克斯坦共和國標準化、計量、認證和貿易檢驗局）管理塔吉克斯坦國家合格評定體系。進口至塔吉克斯坦的電氣設備須符合適用的Tajikstandart注冊標準，並須通過Tajikstandart體系或Tajikstandart認可的檢測和認證機構簽發合格證書或合格聲明。Tajikstandart逐步採納GOST-R衍生標準並與IEC國際標準接軌；電動汽車充電樁適用的具體標準應直接向Tajikstandart或認可合格評定機構確認，因塔吉克斯坦電動汽車特定標準目錄受限於市場初期階段而較為有限。重要說明——非EAEU：塔吉克斯坦不是歐亞經濟聯盟（EAEU）成員。EAC（歐亞合格評定）證書和TR CU（海關聯盟技術法規）路徑是EAEU成員國（俄羅斯、哈薩克斯坦、吉爾吉斯斯坦、亞美尼亞、白俄羅斯）的強制路徑，但不自動賦予在塔吉克斯坦的市場准入資格。EAC標誌不滿足Tajikstandart要求。持有鄰近EAEU市場EAC證書的出口商，在向塔吉克斯坦出口前須單獨獲得Tajikstandart合格評定。

Type: EAC_IN_NON_EAEU
Market: Tajikistan | File: evtj-safety.json
  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.en
  Value: Tajikstandart (the Agency for Standardization, Metrology, Certification and Trade Inspection of the Republic of Tajikistan) is the national standardization and conformity assessment authority. Tajikstandart adopts standards from GOST (the former Soviet standard system) and progressively aligns with IEC standards; conformity declarations or certificates issued through the Tajikstandart system are the domestic market-entry route for electrical equipment. EV chargers as electrical equipment require conformity with applicable Tajikstandart-registered standards. For EV charging equipment, IEC 61851-1:2017 (general requirements for conductive charging systems) and IEC 61851-23:2023 (DC EV supply equipment) represent the IEC baseline that Tajikstandart-aligned projects and technically sophisticated buyers expect. IMPORTANT: Tajikistan is NOT a member of the Eurasian Economic Union (EAEU), and EAC (Eurasian Conformity) certification — the mandatory route for EAEU members such as Russia, Kazakhstan, Kyrgyzstan, Armenia, and Belarus — does NOT automatically cover Tajikistan. EAC certification is not the domestic conformity route for Tajikistan; a Tajikstandart conformity procedure is required. Cold-climate ratings are critically important: major cities (Dushanbe ~750 m elevation) experience winter temperatures of −10 °C to −20 °C, and mountain routes and smaller settlements can reach −30 °C or below. IEC 60068-2-1 cold test and IEC 60721-3 environmental classification at low operating temperature are relevant. Enclosure IP ratings (IP44 minimum for covered AC chargers; IP55 or higher recommended for outdoor installations in alpine conditions) must account for snow ingress and freeze-thaw cycling.

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.zh
  Value: Tajikstandart（塔吉克斯坦共和国标准化、计量、认证和贸易检验局）是国家标准化和合格评定主管机构。Tajikstandart采纳GOST（苏联标准体系）标准，并逐步与IEC标准接轨；通过Tajikstandart体系签发的合格声明或证书是电气设备进入国内市场的路径。电动汽车充电桩作为电气设备，须符合适用的Tajikstandart注册标准。对于电动汽车充电设备，IEC 61851-1:2017（传导充电系统通用要求）和IEC 61851-23:2023（直流电动汽车供电设备）代表了Tajikstandart对齐项目和技术要求较高的买方所预期的IEC基线。重要提示：塔吉克斯坦不是欧亚经济联盟（EAEU）成员，EAC（欧亚合格评定）认证——俄罗斯、哈萨克斯坦、吉尔吉斯斯坦、亚美尼亚和白俄罗斯等EAEU成员的强制路径——不自动覆盖塔吉克斯坦。EAC认证不是塔吉克斯坦的国内合格评定路径，须经Tajikstandart合格评定程序。寒冷气候额定值至关重要：主要城市（杜尚别海拔约750米）冬季气温可达−10°C至−20°C，山区路线和小型聚居点可达−30°C或更低。IEC 60068-2-1低温测试及IEC 60721-3低运行温度环境分类均适用。外壳IP防护等级（有遮蔽交流充电桩至少IP44；高山条件室外安装建议IP55或更高）须考虑积雪渗入和冻融循环。

Chinese EV chargers designed for China are usually frequency-compatible at a basic rating level, as China also uses 50 Hz. The remaining issues are not frequency alone but site voltage tolerance, phase configuration, earthing system (TN-C, TN-S, or TT), power quality, thermal rating, hot-climate operation (Uzbekistan has hot summers), surge environment, and local protection coordination.   Path: [0].requirement_topic.zh

  Path: [0].requirement_topic.zht
  Value: AZSTAND強制符合性認證——亞塞拜疆國家市場准入路徑（非EAEU / 非EAC TR CU）

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.en
  Value: CRITICAL MARKET STRUCTURE NOTE: Azerbaijan is NOT a member of the Eurasian Economic Union (EAEU). EAC conformity marking (EAC TR CU) under the EAEU technical regulations — including TR CU 004/2011 (Low voltage equipment safety) and TR CU 020/2011 (EMC) — does NOT apply to Azerbaijan and does NOT grant Azerbaijan market access. The mandatory conformity route for electrical products in Azerbaijan is through AZSTAND (State Committee for Standardization, Metrology and Patents of Azerbaijan, also referred to as 'Azstandart'). AZSTAND operates mandatory conformity certification for regulated electrical products placed on the Azerbaijan market. PV inverters falling within AZSTAND's current mandatory certification scope require an AZSTAND certificate of conformity before import or sale. The applicant (local importer, authorized representative, or manufacturer) must engage an AZSTAND-accredited conformity assessment body, provide technical documentation and test reports based on applicable AZS national standards (GOST/IEC-derived), and mark the product accordingly. AZSTAND publishes the list of products subject to mandatory certification at azstand.gov.az. The exact mandatory scope for PV inverters must be verified with AZSTAND before shipment as the scope can change.

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.zh
  Value: 关键市场结构说明：阿塞拜疆不是欧亚经济联盟（EAEU）成员国。欧亚经济联盟技术法规下的EAC合格标志（EAC TR CU）——包括TR CU 004/2011（低压设备安全）和TR CU 020/2011（EMC）——不适用于阿塞拜疆，不授予阿塞拜疆市场准入。阿塞拜疆电气产品的强制符合性路径通过AZSTAND（阿塞拜疆标准化、计量和专利国家委员会，亦称「Azstandart」）进行。AZSTAND对投放阿塞拜疆市场的受监管电气产品实施强制符合性认证。属于AZSTAND现行强制认证范围的光伏逆变器在进口或销售前需取得AZSTAND符合性证书。申请人（当地进口商、授权代表或制造商）须委托AZSTAND认可的符合性评估机构，提供基于适用AZS国家标准（GOST/IEC衍生）的技术文件和测试报告，并对产品进行相应标识。AZSTAND在azstand.gov.az发布需强制认证的产品清单。光伏逆变器的确切强制范围须在出货前向AZSTAND核实，因为范围可能发生变化。

  Value: Gap: The primary gap for Chinese PV inverter exporters targeting Azerbaijan is establishing the correct domestic market-access route through AZSTAND — not assuming EAEU EAC TR CU certification applies. Market: Azerbaijan | File: siaz-emc-safety.json
  Path: [1].gap.en
  Value: Chinese GB/T 37408 EMC testing does not satisfy IEC 62920 and IEC 61000-3-2 requirements expected by Azerbaijani project owners and international lenders. Exporters should obtain: (a) IEC 62920 EMC type-test report from an ILAC-accredited laboratory covering the specific inverter model; (b) IEC 61000-3-2 harmonic current emission test report for the model. Because Azerbaijan's nominal grid voltage (220/380 V at 50 Hz) matches China's, retesting under different voltage conditions is generally not required — but confirm this with the project's technical adviser. Separately, confirm with AZSTAND whether mandatory EMC certification is required under domestic AZS or GOST-derived standards for the specific inverter type.

  Path: [1].gap.zh
  Value: 中国GB/T 37408 EMC测试不满足阿塞拜疆项目业主和国际贷款方所期望的IEC 62920和IEC 61000-3-2要求。出口商应取得：（a）来自ILAC认可实验室、涵盖所供应特定逆变器型号的IEC 62920 EMC型式试验报告；（b）该型号的IEC 61000-3-2谐波电流排放测试报告。由于阿塞拜疆标称电网电压（220/380 V 50 Hz）与中国一致，通常不需要在不同电压条件下重新测试——但请向项目技术顾问确认。另请向AZSTAND确认特定逆变器类型是否需要依据国内AZS或GOST标准进行强制EMC认证。

  Path: [1].gap.zht
  Value: 中國GB/T 37408 EMC測試不滿足亞塞拜疆項目業主和國際貸款方所期望的IEC 62920和IEC 61000-3-2要求。出口商應取得：（a）來自ILAC認可實驗室、涵蓋所供應特定逆變器型號的IEC 62920 EMC型式試驗報告；（b）該型號的IEC 61000-3-2諧波電流排放測試報告。由於亞塞拜疆標稱電網電壓（220/380 V 50 Hz）與中國一致，通常不需要在不同電壓條件下重新測試——但請向項目技術顧問確認。另請向AZSTAND確認特定逆變器類型是否需要依據國內AZS或GOST標準進行強制EMC認證。

  Path: [0].requirement_topic.zh

  Path: [0].requirement_topic.zht
  Value: Azerenerji/Azerishig併網要求——50 Hz / 220 V / 380 V獨聯體傳統電網參數及防孤島（IEC 62116 / IEC 61727）

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.en
  Value: Azerbaijan's electricity grid operates at 50 Hz with a CIS-legacy nominal voltage of 220 V single-phase and 380 V three-phase — the same nominal values as China's domestic grid under GB/T 156. Azerenerji is the state-owned generation and transmission company; Azerishig (AzərEnerji subsidiary / distribution arm) operates the distribution and retail network. Grid-connected PV inverters must comply with Azerbaijan's grid-connection technical requirements, which include: (1) IEC 62116 anti-islanding test compliance — inverters must detect loss-of-mains and disconnect within the required time; (2) IEC 61727 (Photovoltaic systems — Characteristics of the utility interface) for grid interface characteristics; (3) frequency and voltage protection thresholds set to Azerishig / Azerenerji network specifications; (4) power quality and harmonic limits per applicable AZS or IEC standards; (5) project-specific grid-connection approval from Azerenerji or Azerishig before energisation. Large-scale projects (e.g., Masdar Garadagh 230 MW, ACWA Power projects) follow IEC standards and lender specifications (EBRD, IFC) regardless of whether local minimums require them. IMPORTANT: The nominal CIS 220/380 V at 50 Hz grid means re-parameterisation risk versus Chinese factory firmware is low compared to markets with different nominal voltages, but Azerbaijan grid-operator approval and project-specific protection settings remain mandatory — China domestic grid-connection approval does not transfer.

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.zh
  Value: 阿塞拜疆电网以50 Hz运行，独联体传统标称电压为单相220 V、三相380 V——与中国依据GB/T 156的国内电网标称值相同。Azerenerji为国有发电和输电公司；Azerishig（Azerenerji子公司/配电部门）运营配电和零售网络。并网光伏逆变器须符合阿塞拜疆并网技术要求，包括：（1）IEC 62116防孤岛测试合规——逆变器须在规定时间内检测电网失电并断开；（2）IEC 61727（光伏系统——公用电力接口特性）对电网接口特性的规定；（3）频率和电压保护阈值须按Azerishig/Azerenerji电网规格设定；（4）符合适用AZS或IEC标准的电能质量和谐波限值；（5）送电前须取得Azerenerji或Azerishig的项目专属并网批准。大型项目（如Masdar Garadagh 230 MW、ACWA Power项目）无论当地最低要求是否要求，均须遵循IEC标准和贷款方（欧洲复兴开发银行、国际金融公司）规格。重要提示：独联体标称220/380 V 50 Hz电网意味着与中国出厂固件相比重新参数化风险较低，但阿塞拜疆电网运营商批准和项目专属保护设置仍为强制要求——中国国内并网审批不能转移。

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.zht

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.en
  Value: Georgia's grid-connection technical requirements for solar PV inverters are governed by the Georgian National Energy and Water Supply Regulatory Commission (GNERC) and the transmission system operator Georgian State Electrosystem (GSE). Distribution is operated by Telasi (Tbilisi) and Energo-Pro Georgia (regions). Georgia's grid operates at 50 Hz, single-phase 220 V, three-phase 380 V — a CIS-legacy parameter set shared with China. Under Georgia's Deep and Comprehensive Free Trade Area (DCFTA) agreement with the EU, Georgia is progressively aligning technical regulations with EU/IEC standards. Key grid-connection requirements for PV inverters include: (1) IEC 62116 anti-islanding test evidence — inverters must detect loss of mains and disconnect within the required window; (2) IEC 61727 (Photovoltaic systems — Characteristics of the utility interface) compliance for grid-interface parameters; (3) IEC 61000-3-2 harmonic current emission limits; (4) firmware and protection relay settings validated against Georgia's 220/380 V, 50 Hz grid parameters. Grid-connection applicants must submit technical documentation to GSE or the relevant distribution operator (Telasi / Energo-Pro Georgia) and obtain GNERC-regulated connection approval.

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.zh
  Value: 格鲁吉亚太阳能光伏逆变器并网技术要求由格鲁吉亚国家能源和供水监管委员会（GNERC）及输电系统运营商格鲁吉亚国家电力系统（GSE）管理。配电由Telasi（第比利斯）和Energo-Pro Georgia（其他地区）运营。格鲁吉亚电网运行参数为50 Hz、单相220 V、三相380 V——与中国相同的苏联遗留参数集。根据格鲁吉亚与欧盟签订的《深入和全面自由贸易协定》（DCFTA），格鲁吉亚正逐步将技术法规与欧盟/IEC标准对接。光伏逆变器并网的主要要求包括：（1）IEC 62116防孤岛测试证据——逆变器须在规定时间内检测电网失电并断开；（2）IEC 61727（光伏系统——公用电网接口特性）电网接口参数合规；（3）IEC 61000-3-2谐波电流排放限值；（4）针对格鲁吉亚220/380 V、50 Hz电网参数验证的固件和保护继电器整定。并网申请方须向GSE或相关配电运营商（Telasi / Energo-Pro Georgia）提交技术文件，并取得GNERC监管的接入审批。

  Value: China's primary voluntary standard for PV grid-connected inverter safety is GB/T 37408-2021 (Technical Requirements for Photovoltaic Grid-Connected Inverters), which covers classification, environmental conditions, safety, electrical performance, EMC, and markings.   Value: PV inverter deployment in Kyrgyzstan is a product-compliance and project-connection question.   Path: [0].gap.en
  Value: Chinese GB/T 37408 EMC testing does not satisfy Tajikstandart IEC 61000-series requirements or World Bank / ADB project procurement EMC evidence requirements for Tajikistan. Exporters should obtain: (a) IEC 61000-3-2 harmonic current emission test report from an ILAC-accredited laboratory for the specific inverter model; (b) IEC 61000-3-3 voltage fluctuation and flicker test report where applicable; (c) IEC 61000-6-2 immunity test report for the industrial environment; (d) for utility-scale donor/lender projects: IEC 62920 EMC type-test report. These reports should be specific to the power rating and configuration of the inverter model supplied to the Tajikistan project. Note: because Tajikistan's nominal grid voltage (220/380 V at 50 Hz) matches China's nominal voltage, retesting solely for grid voltage conditions is less likely to be required than in markets with different nominal voltages (e.g., 240/415 V Qatar). However, confirm with the project engineer whether Barqi Tojik actual voltage tolerance conditions affect EMC test result applicability.

  Path: [0].target_requirement.summary.en
  Value: Tajikistan's national conformity system is administered by Tajikstandart (the Agency for Standardization, Metrology, Certification and Trade Inspection). Electrical and energy equipment sold or installed in Tajikistan must obtain Tajikstandart conformity certification (a Tajikistan Certificate of Conformity or Declaration of Conformity under the national system). CRITICAL DISTINCTION: Tajikistan is NOT a member of the Eurasian Economic Union (EAEU) — it holds observer/candidate status only. EAC marking (issued under EAEU Technical Regulations / TR CU) does NOT by itself authorise market access in Tajikistan. Exporters who hold EAC certificates obtained for Kazakhstan, Kyrgyzstan, Armenia, or Russia cannot rely on those certificates for Tajikistan market access. The applicable conformity route is domestic Tajikstandart certification, referencing Tajik national standards (ST RT) or adopted GOST/IEC standards. Requirements for specific inverter power classes should be confirmed directly with Tajikstandart before shipment.

Type: GRID_DIFFERENCE
Market: Tajikistan | File: sitj-grid.json
  Path: [1].requirement_topic.en
  Value: Barqi Tojik Grid-Connection and Anti-Islanding — IEC 62116, IEC 61727, 50 Hz / 220/380 V Settings

  Path: [1].requirement_topic.zh
  Value: Barqi Tojik并网与防孤岛——IEC 62116、IEC 61727、50 Hz / 220/380 V参数

  Value: Barqi Tojik併網與防孤島——IEC 62116、IEC 61727、50 Hz / 220/380 V參數

  Path: [1].target_requirement.summary.en
  Value: Barqi Tojik (Tajikistan's state vertically-integrated electricity utility, operating under the Ministry of Energy and Water Resources) sets grid-connection technical requirements for distributed and utility-scale solar PV inverters. Tajikistan's electricity grid operates at 50 Hz, 220 V single-phase and 380 V three-phase — the same nominal voltage as China's GB/T 156 grid, but grid stability, voltage tolerance, and protection relay settings must be validated against Barqi Tojik's actual operating conditions rather than Chinese grid parameters. Key grid-connection requirements applied in Barqi Tojik and donor/lender (World Bank, ADB) project specifications include: (1) IEC 62116 anti-islanding test — inverters must detect loss of mains and disconnect within 2 seconds; (2) IEC 61727 (Photovoltaic systems — Characteristics of the utility interface) for grid interface performance; (3) firmware protection thresholds and reconnection delays validated against Tajikistan's 50 Hz, 220/380 V grid and actual Barqi Tojik operating conditions; (4) IEC 61000-3-2 harmonic current emission limits. Utility-scale and donor-financed projects may also require Low Voltage Ride-Through (LVRT) evidence per IEC TS 62910 or lender technical specifications.

  Path: [1].target_requirement.summary.zh
  Value: Barqi Tojik（塔吉克斯坦国家垂直一体化电力公用事业，隶属能源和水资源部）规定了分布式和公用事业规模太阳能光伏逆变器的并网技术要求。塔吉克斯坦电网运行参数为50 Hz、单相220 V、三相380 V——与中国GB/T 156电网名义电压相同，但电网稳定性、电压容差及保护继电器整定须依据Barqi Tojik实际运行条件进行验证，而非中国电网参数。Barqi Tojik及援助方/贷款方（世界银行、亚开行）项目规格中适用的主要并网要求包括：（1）IEC 62116防孤岛测试——逆变器须在2秒内检测电网失电并断开；（2）IEC 61727（光伏系统——电网接口特性）用于电网接口性能；（3）针对塔吉克斯坦50 Hz、220/380 V电网及Barqi Tojik实际运行条件验证固件保护阈值和重连延迟；（4）IEC 61000-3-2谐波电流排放限值。公用事业规模和援助方资助项目还可能要求符合IEC TS 62910或贷款方技术规格的低电压穿越（LVRT）证据。

  Path: [1].target_requirement.summary.zht
  Value: Barqi Tojik（塔吉克斯坦國家垂直一體化電力公用事業，隸屬能源和水資源部）規定了分散式和公用事業規模太陽能光伏逆變器的併網技術要求。塔吉克斯坦電網運行參數為50 Hz、單相220 V、三相380 V——與中國GB/T 156電網名義電壓相同，但電網穩定性、電壓容差及保護繼電器整定須依據Barqi Tojik實際運行條件進行驗證，而非中國電網參數。Barqi Tojik及援助方/貸款方（世界銀行、亞開行）項目規格中適用的主要併網要求包括：（1）IEC 62116防孤島測試——逆變器須在2秒內偵測電網失電並斷開；（2）IEC 61727（光伏系統——電網接口特性）用於電網接口性能；（3）針對塔吉克斯坦50 Hz、220/380 V電網及Barqi Tojik實際運行條件驗證韌體保護閾值和重連延遲；（4）IEC 61000-3-2諧波電流排放限值。公用事業規模和援助方資助項目還可能要求符合IEC TS 62910或貸款方技術規格的低電壓穿越（LVRT）證據。

  Path: [1].cn_common_equivalent.summary.en
  Value: Chinese grid-connection evidence commonly includes GB/T 19964-2024 (Technical Requirements for Connecting Photovoltaic Power Station to Power System, applicable to utility-scale PV via 10 kV and above), NB/T 32004-2018 (inverter technical specifications), and domestic anti-islanding test results under GB/T 37408.   Path: [1].cn_common_equivalent.standards_or_laws[1]

  Path: [1].gap.en
  Value: Gap: While Tajikistan shares China's 50 Hz / 220/380 V nominal voltage, Chinese GB/T grid-connection documents do not satisfy Barqi Tojik or donor/lender requirements.
